<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>To the Company's Shareholders: 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This information statement is 
being furnished to the holders of common stock of Clayton Williams 
Energy,&nbsp;Inc., a Delaware corporation (the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), to provide our 
shareholders with notice of corporate action expected to occur on or about 
August&nbsp;30, 2016.
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Certain
of our shareholders holding a majority of our outstanding common stock, par 
value $0.10 per share (our "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>common stock</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>"), approved
the issuance of 5,051,100 shares of common stock by written consent in lieu of a
meeting as permitted by the Delaware General Corporation Law and our corporate 
bylaws. The common stock will be sold in
a private placement to affiliates of Ares Management&nbsp;LLC in exchange for 
$150.0&nbsp;million in cash in accordance with a common stock purchase agreement
between the Company and the purchaser
parties thereto, dated July&nbsp;22, 2016. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B>WE ARE NOT ASKING 
YOU FOR A PROXY AND YOU ARE REQUESTED NOT TO SEND US A PROXY  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We are furnishing this 
information statement to provide you with important information about this 
matter. Please read this information statement carefully. We
thank you for your continued support. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> INFORMATION 
STATEMENT AND NOTICE OF ACTIONS TAKEN WITHOUT A MEETING  </B></FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><I>
<!-- COMMAND=ADD_LINERULETXT,NOSHADE  COLOR="#000000" SIZE="1.0PT" WIDTH="26%" 
ALIGN="CENTER" -->
<HR NOSHADE  COLOR="#000000" SIZE="1.0PT" WIDTH="26%" ALIGN="CENTER" >

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> <A 
NAME="da17301_summary"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_da17301_1"> </A>
  SUMMARY    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Clayton Williams 
Energy,&nbsp;Inc., a Delaware corporation, with its principal executive offices 
located at 6 Desta Drive,
Suite&nbsp;6500, Midland, Texas 79705-5510, is furnishing this information 
statement and notice of actions taken without a meeting to our shareholders in 
connection with the approval by our majority
shareholders by written consent of the matters described below. Unless the 
context requires otherwise, references to the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>,"
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>CWEI</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>," "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>our</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>," "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>us</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>,"
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>we</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" and like terms refer to 
Clayton Williams Energy,&nbsp;Inc. and its consolidated subsidiaries. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Copies of this information 
statement are being mailed on or about August&nbsp;8, 2016, to the holders of 
record at the close of business on July&nbsp;22, 2016 (the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Record Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). As of the close 
of business on the Record Date, there were 12,169,536&nbsp;shares of our common 
stock, par value $0.10 per share
("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>common stock</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), issued and 
outstanding.
</FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B>WE ARE NOT ASKING 
YOU FOR A PROXY AND YOU ARE REQUESTED NOT TO SEND US A PROXY  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All corporate approvals 
by or on behalf of the Company required for these matters have been obtained. 
This information statement is furnished solely for the
purpose of informing our shareholders of these corporate actions in the manner 
required by Regulation&nbsp;14C of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as 
amended (the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Exchange Act</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), and 
Section&nbsp;228(e) of the Delaware General Corporation Law (the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>DGCL</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Actions by Written Consent  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The corporate actions 
described in this information statement were approved by the written consent of 
the holders of a majority of our
outstanding common stock in
accordance with the DGCL and our corporate bylaws (the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Bylaws</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). Specifically, on July&nbsp;22, 2016,
(1)&nbsp;Clayton&nbsp;W. Williams, Jr., the
Chief Executive Officer of the Company and certain related entities, 
(2)&nbsp;The Williams Children's' Partnership,&nbsp;Ltd., a Delaware limited 
partnership of which Mr.&nbsp;Williams' adult
children are the limited partners, and Mel&nbsp;G. Riggs, the Company's 
President, is the sole general partner ("</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>WCPL</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") and
(3)&nbsp;Mr.&nbsp;Riggs, who together hold a majority of the voting power of our
outstanding common stock (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Majority 
Shareholders</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), approved by
written consent the issuance of an aggregate of 5,051,100&nbsp;shares of common 
stock in a private placement transaction to affiliates of Ares 
Management&nbsp;LLC
("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Ares</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>," and such affiliate 
funds, the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Purchasers</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") in 
exchange for $150.0&nbsp;million in cash,
pursuant to the Common Stock Purchase Agreement, dated July&nbsp;22, 2016, by 
and between the Company and the Purchasers (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Common 
Stock Purchase
Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). As of the close of business on such date, 
there were 12,169,536&nbsp;shares of our common stock issued and outstanding, 
and the Majority Shareholders approved
the written consent with approximately 50.3% of our issued and outstanding 
common stock. See "Security Ownership of Certain Beneficial Owners and 
Management" for additional information about the
beneficial ownership of our common stock by our Majority Shareholders. 
</FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>1</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>

<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
NYSE Listing Requirements and Need for Shareholder Approval  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The corporate actions 
described in this information statement required shareholder approval from the 
holders of our outstanding common
stock because our common stock is traded on the New York Stock Exchange 
("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>NYSE</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). We are subject to 
Rule&nbsp;312 of the NYSE Listed Company Manual
("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Rule&nbsp;312</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), which requires
that we obtain shareholder approval in certain circumstances, including before 
(1)&nbsp;issuing shares of common
stock in excess of 5% of our outstanding common stock prior to such issuance to 
a substantial security holder, including, in this instance, the Purchasers, 
(2)&nbsp;issuing shares of common stock in
excess of 20% of our outstanding common stock prior to such issuance and 
(3)&nbsp;issuing shares of common stock that will result in a change of control 
of the Company under the general
interpretations of the NYSE. We expect the 5,051,100&nbsp;shares of common stock
to be issued in connection with the Common Stock Purchase Agreement to represent
approximately 41.5% of our
outstanding common stock immediately prior to such issuance pursuant to the 
calculation rules required by the NYSE. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The issuance of the common stock
will occur upon the closing of the Common Stock Purchase Agreement, which is 
expected to occur on or about August&nbsp;30, 2016, at least twenty days
after this information statement is mailed to our shareholders.
</FONT></P>

SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> the

under existing agreements; </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> the 
uncertainty inherent in estimating proved oil and gas reserves and in projecting
future rates of production and timing of
development expenditures; </FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> drilling 
and other operating risks; </FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> hurricanes
and other weather conditions; </FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> lack of 
availability of goods and services; </FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> regulatory
and environmental risks associated with drilling and production activities; 
</FONT> <FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> the 
adverse effects of changes in applicable tax, environmental and other regulatory
legislation; and </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2>
<BR><BR></FONT></DD><DT style='font-family:times;margin-bottom:-11pt;'><FONT 
SIZE=2>&#149;</FONT></DT><DD style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2> the other 
risks described in our Form&nbsp;10-K for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2015.
</FONT></DD></DL>
</UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Reserve
engineering is a subjective process of estimating underground accumulations of 
oil and gas that cannot be measured in an exact way. The accuracy of any reserve
estimate depends
on the quality of available data and the interpretation of that data by 
geological engineers. In addition, the results of drilling, testing and 
production activities may justify revisions of estimates
that were made previously. If significant, these revisions would change the 
schedule of any further production and development
drilling. Accordingly, reserve estimates are generally different from the 
quantities of oil and gas that are ultimately recovered. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As
previously discussed, should one or more of the risks or uncertainties described
above or elsewhere in our Form&nbsp;10-K for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 
2015 and in this
information statement occur, or should underlying assumptions prove incorrect, 
our actual results and plans could differ materially from those expressed in any
forward-looking statements. Readers are
cautioned not to place undue reliance on forward-looking statements, which speak
only as of the date hereof. We specifically disclaim all responsibility to 
publicly update or revise any
forward-looking statements or any information contained in a forward-looking
statement or any forward-looking statement in its entirety after the date made, 
whether as a result of new information,
future events or otherwise, except as required by law. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All
forward-looking statements attributable to us are expressly qualified in their 
entirety by this cautionary statement. </FONT></P>

<A NAME="toc_dc17301_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  ACTIONS BY WRITTEN CONSENT    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Background  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Previous Ares Transaction  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On March&nbsp;15, 2016, 
in connection with a $350,000,000 term loan from certain affiliates of Ares, we 
issued warrants to purchase
2,251,364&nbsp;shares of common stock to affiliates of Ares at an exercise price
of $22.00 per share, which represented approximately 18.5% of the Company's 
shares of common stock outstanding prior
to issuance (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Previous Ares 
Transaction</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). The warrants expire on March&nbsp;15, 
2026. Subsequently, Ares and its affiliates independently
purchased additional shares of our common stock in the open market, and Ares is 
currently a 22.8% beneficial owner of the common stock of the Company, as 
further described under "Security Ownership of
Certain Beneficial Owners and Management." </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Additionally,
in connection with the Previous Ares Transaction, we designated and issued to 
Ares and certain of its affiliates (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Special 
Preferred
Holders</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") 3,500&nbsp;shares of special voting preferred 
stock, $0.10 par value per share (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Special Preferred 
Stock</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"),
granting them the right to elect two directors to the Board. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Common Stock Purchase Agreement  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On or about June&nbsp;6, 
2016, Ares approached the management of the Company to discuss its willingness 
to contribute substantial
equity capital to the Company. On July&nbsp;6, 2016, the board of directors of 
the Company (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Board</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>")
established a transaction committee (the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Transaction Committee</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") to 
evaluate, negotiate, determine the advisability of and determine whether to 
recommend approval of the Private Placement
(defined below) to the Board. The Transaction Committee consisted of solely 
independent and disinterested directors. The members of the Transaction 
Committee were Jordan&nbsp;R. Smith,
Davis&nbsp;L. Ford and Ted Gray, Jr. The Transaction Committee retained Goldman,
Sachs&nbsp;&amp;&nbsp;Co. as financial advisor and Potter Anderson&nbsp;&amp; 
Corroon&nbsp;LLP as legal counsel. On
July&nbsp;22, 2016, the Transaction Committee recommended, and the Board 
approved, the issuance of an aggregate of 5,051,100&nbsp;shares of common stock 
(the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Purchased
Shares</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") in a private placement transaction to the 
Purchasers in exchange for an aggregate amount of $150.0&nbsp;million in cash 
pursuant to the terms and conditions of the
Common Stock Purchase Agreement (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Private 
Placement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The closing of the Private 
Placement (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Closing</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), which 
is expected to occur on or about August&nbsp;30, 2016, is subject to certain
conditions, including, among others, (1)&nbsp;clearance by the SEC of this 
information statement, (2)&nbsp;expiration or early termination of the waiting 
period under the Hart-Scott-Rodino
Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended, and (3)&nbsp;authorization by 
the NYSE of listing of the Purchased Shares.
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Purchase Agreement contains customary representations, warranties and covenants 
of the Company and the Purchasers, and the parties have agreed to indemnify each
other against certain
losses resulting from breaches of their respective representations, warranties 
and covenants. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Purchase Agreement may be terminated under certain circumstances, including 
(1)&nbsp;if a statute, rule, order, decree or regulation is enacted that 
permanently prohibits the
consummation of the transactions contemplated by the Purchase Agreement, or 
(2)&nbsp;if the Closing has not occurred by October&nbsp;20, 2016. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
foregoing summary describes certain material terms of the Common Stock Purchase 
Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby but is not intended to be 
complete and is
qualified in its entirety by the text of the Common Stock Purchase Agreement 
attached as </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Annex&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> to this 
information statement. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>5</FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Stockholder Agreement  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, upon the 
closing of the Private Placement, pursuant to a Stockholder Agreement between 
the Company and Ares, on behalf of
the Purchasers, to be entered into pursuant to the Common Stock Purchase 
Agreement (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Stockholder Agreement</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>"), the Purchasers will receive the right
to designate one director nominee for election to the Board, subject to approval
by the Nominating and Governance Committee of the Board from and after the 
Closing. On July&nbsp;22, 2016, the Board
amended our Bylaws to allow the Board to set the number of directors pursuant to
a Board resolution. The Board has also agreed to increase the size of the Board 
from seven to nine directors upon
Closing. The Special Preferred Holders, as the sole holders of the Special 
Preferred Stock, pursuant to the Certificate of Designation of the Special 
Preferred Stock filed with the Secretary of State
of the State of Delaware on March&nbsp;15, 2016, have the right to approve 
increases in the number of directors. On July&nbsp;22, 2016, the Special 
Preferred Holders approved the proposed increase
in the number of directors in connection with the signing of the Common Stock 
Purchase Agreement. The Board also approved an amendment to our Bylaws to 
designate the Delaware Court of Chancery as the
exclusive forum for certain disputes relating to the Company, unless we consent 
in writing to the selection of an alternative forum. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In
addition, pursuant to the Stockholder Agreement, Ares, the Purchasers and their 
controlled affiliates (together, the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Shareholder
Group</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") will agree to (1)&nbsp;a limitation on the 
aggregate number of shares of
common stock that the Shareholder Group may beneficially own on a fully-diluted 
basis, which may not exceed 45% of the outstanding common stock and the shares 
of common stock issuable upon full
exercise of the warrants of the Company owned by Ares or its affiliates (the 
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Ownership Cap</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") and 
(2)&nbsp;procedures for reviewing and approving
future material related party transactions, if any, between the Company and any 
member of the Shareholder Group. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Stockholder Agreement will terminate under certain circumstances, including at 
such time as the Shareholder Group no longer beneficially owns 30% of the 
outstanding common stock
(calculated on a fully-diluted basis). However, the Ownership Cap will survive 
any termination of the Stockholder Agreement until such time as (1)(a) the 
Shareholder Group ceases to own at least 20%
of the outstanding common stock (calculated on a fully-diluted basis), and 
(b)&nbsp;that certain Credit Agreement (defined below) has been terminated or no
amounts are otherwise owed or outstanding
to Ares or its affiliates under the Credit Agreement or (2)&nbsp;the Company 
files for bankruptcy. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
foregoing summary describes certain material terms of the proposed Stockholder 
Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby but is not intended to be 
complete and is qualified
in its entirety by the text of the Form of Stockholder Agreement attached as 
Exhibit&nbsp;A to </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Annex&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> to
this Information Statement. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Amendment No.&nbsp;2 to Credit Agreement  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On July&nbsp;22, 2016, we
entered into an Amendment No.&nbsp;2 to Credit Agreement (the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Term Loan
Amendment</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), pursuant to which the Credit Agreement, 
dated as of March&nbsp;8, 2016 (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Credit 
Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), among the
Company, certain subsidiaries of the Company, as Guarantors, the Lenders party 
thereto and Wilmington Trust, National Association, as Administrative Agent, 
will be amended, effective at the Closing,
upon the satisfaction of certain conditions, including the issuance of the 
Purchased Shares as contemplated by the Common Stock Purchase Agreement. Upon 
the effectiveness of the Term Loan Amendment,
the Term Loan Amendment will, among other things, (1)&nbsp;provide exceptions to
the consent and mandatory prepayment provisions under the Credit Agreement for 
certain asset sales and
(2)&nbsp;increase the basket for permitted prepayments, repurchases, 
redemptions, defeasances or discharges of our senior notes by the amount of the 
funds raised by the Private Placement, future
equity raises and certain asset sales. </FONT></P>

is qualified in its
entirety by the text of the Term Loan Amendment attached as </FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Annex&nbsp;B</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> to this Information Statement. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B><I>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Registration Rights  </I></B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In connection with the 
Previous Ares Transaction, we entered into a registration rights agreement with 
affiliates of Ares dated
March&nbsp;15, 2016 (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Registration Rights 
Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). The Registration Rights Agreement covers 
(1)&nbsp;the common stock issuable upon exercise
of warrants issued in the Previous Ares Transaction and (2)&nbsp;other common 
stock owned by Ares or its affiliates, including the Purchased Shares 
(collectively, the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Registrable Shares</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). Pursuant 
to the Registration Rights Agreement, and subject to limitations set forth 
therein, the Company is required to use
commercially reasonable efforts to effect up to five registrations with the SEC 
with respect to the registration of the offer of all Registrable Shares that the
Purchasers request to be registered.
Pursuant to the Registration Rights Agreement, the Company has also granted the 
Purchasers piggyback registration rights on the terms and conditions set forth 
therein. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
foregoing summary describes certain material terms of the Registration Rights 
Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby but is not intended to be 
complete and is qualified
in its entirety by the text of the Registration Rights Agreement attached as 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Annex&nbsp;C</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> to this information 
statement. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
NYSE Rules  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Because our common stock 
is traded on the NYSE, we are subject to Rule&nbsp;312 of the NYSE Listed 
Company Manual
("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Rule&nbsp;312</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). 
Rules&nbsp;312.03(b), 312.03(c) and 312.03(d) of the NYSE Listed Company Manual 
require shareholder approval, respectively, in
certain circumstances, including (1)&nbsp;prior to the issuance of common stock 
or securities convertible into or exercisable for common stock in a transaction 
or series of transactions in excess of
5% of the voting power outstanding before the issuance of such stock or
securities convertible into or exercisable for common stock to a "substantial 
security holder" (which term includes Ares and the
Purchasers), (2)&nbsp;prior to the issuance of common stock or securities 
convertible into or exercisable for common stock if (a)&nbsp;the common stock 
has, or will have upon issuance, voting
power equal to or in excess of 20% of the voting power outstanding before the 
issuance of such stock or securities convertible into or exercisable for common 
stock, or (b)&nbsp;the number of shares
of common stock to be issued is, or will be upon issuance, equal to or in excess
of 20% of the number of shares of common stock outstanding before the issuance 
of the common stock or securities
convertible into or exercisable for common stock and (3)&nbsp;prior to an 
issuance that will result in a change of control under the general 
interpretations of the NYSE. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We
expect the Purchased Shares to constitute approximately 41.5% of our outstanding
common stock immediately prior to such issuance pursuant to the calculation 
rules required by the
NYSE. Shareholder approval of the Private Placement may be required under 
Rule&nbsp;312, because (1)&nbsp;the issuance of the Purchased Shares will result
in the sale of common stock to Ares and
its affiliate Purchasers, considered a substantial security holder of the 
Company, in an amount greater than 5% of the voting power outstanding before the
issuance of such stock, (2)&nbsp;the
issuance of the Purchased Shares will be in excess of 20% of the voting power 
and number of shares of common stock outstanding before the issuance and 
(3)&nbsp;the issuance may result in a change of
control under the general interpretations of the NYSE. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Action by Written Consent  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pursuant to 
Section&nbsp;228 of the DGCL and Section&nbsp;2.11 of our Bylaws, any action 
required or permitted to be taken at any
annual or special meeting of shareholders may be taken without a meeting, 
without prior notice and without a vote of shareholders, if a consent or 
consents in writing, </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>7</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=3,SEQ=10,EFW="2229331",CP="CLAYTON WILLIAMS ENERGY, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=869761,FOLIO='7',FILE='DISK129:
[16ZBW1.16ZBW17301]DC17301A.;5',USER='CHE108062',CD=';3-AUG-2016;01:03' -->
<A NAME="page_dc17301_1_8"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A HREF="#bg17301a_main_toc">Table of
Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>setting
forth the action so taken, is signed by the holders of outstanding stock having
not less than the minimum number of votes that would be necessary to authorize 
or take such action at a meeting
at which all shares entitled to vote thereon were present and voted. On 
July&nbsp;22, 2016, Mr.&nbsp;Williams, Mr.&nbsp;Riggs and WCPL, together voting 
6,123,886&nbsp;shares of our common
stock, representing approximately 50.3% of the voting power of our outstanding 
shares of common stock, approved by written consent (the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Written
Consent</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") the issuance of the shares of common stock to 
the Purchasers in the Private Placement as required by Rule&nbsp;312. We 
concurrently entered into the Common Stock
Purchase Agreement with the Purchasers, pursuant to which we agreed to issue an 
aggregate of 5,051,100 shares of our common stock to the Purchasers for a 
purchase price of approximately $29.70 per
share, representing gross proceeds to us of $150.0&nbsp;million (before 
deducting our offering expenses), and also agreed to enter into the Stockholder 
Agreement. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
No Further Shareholder Action Needed  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;">
<FONT SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As a result of the 
Written Consent, the requisite shareholder approval of the issuance of the 
Purchased Shares in the Private Placement
has been received as required under Rule&nbsp;312. Accordingly, all corporate 
approvals by or on behalf of the Company required for the matters referred to 
herein have been obtained and no further
votes will be needed. We expect that the issuance of the Purchased Shares to the
Purchasers in the Private Placement will occur on the date that all of the 
closing conditions set forth in the Common
Stock Purchase Agreement have been satisfied or waived, which is expected to be 
on or about August&nbsp;30, 2016. The Board does not intend to solicit any 
proxies or consents in connection with the
foregoing actions.
</FONT>
</P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This
information statement is furnished solely for the purpose of informing 
shareholders regarding the actions taken by the Written Consent and is being 
provided pursuant to the
requirements of Rule&nbsp;14c-2 promulgated under Section&nbsp;13 of the 
Exchange Act and Section&nbsp;228(e) of the DGCL. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Reasons for the Actions Taken  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We agreed to sell an 
aggregate of 5,051,100&nbsp;shares of common stock for an aggregate price of 
$150.0&nbsp;million. We believe
that the Private Placement will strengthen our balance sheet and provide an 
opportunity to reduce leverage and accelerate our drilling program. We intend to
use the net proceeds received from the
Private Placement to tender for a portion of our 7.75% Senior Notes due 2019 
(the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Tender Offer</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") and for 
general corporate purposes, which may include
developmental drilling on our 65,000 net acre position in the core of the 
southern Delaware Basin. There are no assurances that we will consummate the 
Tender Offer or that any of the 7.75% Senior
Notes due 2019 will be tendered in the Tender Offer. If for any reason the 
Tender Offer is not completed, we intend to use all of the net proceeds from the
Private Placement for general corporate
purposes. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;;margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><FONT 
SIZE=2><B>
<!-- COMMAND=STYLE_ADDED,"margin-left:10.0pt;text-indent:-10.0pt;" -->
Effects of the Proposed Issuance  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The issuance of a 
significant amount of common stock may have a positive or negative effect on the
price of our common stock. The
issuance will also result in significant dilution to our shareholders and result
in our shareholders having a smaller percentage interest in the
voting power, liquidation value and aggregate book value of the Company. In 
connection with the Previous Ares Transaction, we granted registration rights to
permit the public resale of shares of
common stock acquired by Ares and its affiliates. The influx of such a 
substantial number of shares of common stock into the public market could have a
significant negative effect on the trading price
of our common stock. As of July&nbsp;22, 2016, 12,169,536&nbsp;shares of common 
stock were outstanding, and 2,251,364&nbsp;shares of common stock were subject 
to registration rights previously
granted to Ares in connection with the issuance of the warrants in the Previous 
Ares Transaction. An additional 5,051,100&nbsp;shares of common stock will be 
outstanding upon the closing of the
Private Placement, and 7,302,464&nbsp;shares of common stock will be subject to 
registration rights. Issuance of these shares of common stock will substantially
dilute the ownership </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>8</FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>
<!-- ZEQ.=4,SEQ=11,EFW="2229331",CP="CLAYTON WILLIAMS ENERGY, 
INC.",DN="1",CHK=909289,FOLIO='8',FILE='DISK129:
[16ZBW1.16ZBW17301]DC17301A.;5',USER='CHE108062',CD=';3-AUG-2016;01:03' -->
<A NAME="page_dc17301_1_9"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A HREF="#bg17301a_main_toc">Table of
Contents</A></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2>interests
of our existing shareholders who are not participating in the Private Placement.
The potential issuance of such additional shares of common stock may create 
downward pressure on the trading
price of our common stock. In a volatile market, we may experience wide 
fluctuations in the market price of our common stock. These fluctuations may 
also have a negative effect on the market price of
our common stock. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="dc17301_no_dissenter_s_rights"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_dc17301_2"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  NO DISSENTER'S RIGHTS    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The corporate action 
described in this information statement will not afford to shareholders the 
opportunity to dissent from the
actions described herein or to receive an agreed or judicially appraised value 
for their shares. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="dc17301_interest_of_certain_persons_in_the_actions_taken"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_dc17301_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  INTEREST OF CERTAIN PERSONS IN THE ACTIONS TAKEN   
<BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the Previous Ares 
Transaction, on March&nbsp;15, 2016, in connection with a $350&nbsp;million term
loan from Ares, we issued
warrants to purchase 2,251,364&nbsp;shares of common stock to affiliates of 
Ares, which represented approximately 18.5% of the Company's shares of common 
stock outstanding prior to issuance. Ares
has independently purchased additional shares of our common stock in the open 
market and is currently a 22.8% beneficial owner of the common stock of the 
Company, as further described under "Security
Ownership of Certain Beneficial Owners and Management." Additionally, in 
connection with the Previous Ares Transaction, we designated and issued to Ares 
and its affiliates 3,500&nbsp;shares of
Special Preferred Stock, granting them the right to appoint two directors to the
Board. In 2016, Ares appointed Nathan&nbsp;W. Walton, a Partner in the Private 
Equity Group of Ares,
and P.&nbsp;Scott Martin, the Founder, Chief Executive Officer and Senior 
Partner of BlackBrush Oil&nbsp;&amp; Gas,&nbsp;LP, to the Board. Funds managed 
by Ares also own a controlling interest in
BlackBrush. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After
the closing of the Private Placement, Ares will be the beneficial owner of 
8,344,869&nbsp;shares of common stock, representing approximately 42.9% of the 
Company's outstanding
shares of common stock on a fully-diluted basis. Pursuant to the Registration 
Rights Agreement entered into in connection with the Previous Ares Transaction, 
Ares and its affiliates will have
registration rights with regard to all shares of common stock that they own. In 
connection with the Stockholder Agreement and as a result of the Previous Ares 
Transaction, Ares will also have the
right to appoint two out of nine directors to our Board, and the ability to 
designate an additional nominee to our Board, subject to approval by the 
Nominating and Corporate Governance Committee.
Additionally, the terms of the Stockholder Agreement will limit Ares and its 
affiliates from making any additional acquisitions of common stock that would 
cause its beneficial ownership on a fully
diluted basis to exceed 45% of the common stock of the Company, and will require
approval by a majority of the unaffiliated Board members or by a majority of the
Company's shareholders (excluding Ares
and its affiliates) for any related party transaction between the Company and 
Ares and its affiliates. After the closing of the Private Placement, Ares will 
be the beneficial owner of
8,344,869&nbsp;shares of common stock, representing approximately 42.9% for 
purposes of the Ownership Cap. See "Actions by Written 
Consent&#151;Background&#151;Stockholder Agreement"
and "&#151;Registration Rights" above for additional information. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For
additional information about the interests of our directors and officers in the 
Private Placement, see "Security Ownership of Certain Beneficial Owners and 
Management." </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="de17301_where_you_can_find_more_information"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_de17301_2"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  WHERE YOU CAN FIND MORE INFORMATION    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;We file periodic reports,
proxy and information statements and other information with the SEC in 
accordance with the requirements of
the Exchange Act. Our SEC filings are available to the public over the Internet 
at the SEC's web site at www.sec.gov. You also may read and copy any document we
file at the SEC's public reference room
in Washington, D.C. Please call the SEC at 1-800-SEC-0330 for further 
information about the public reference room. Our common stock is listed and 
traded on the NYSE under the trading symbol "CWEI." </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="de17301_shareholders_sharing_an_address"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_de17301_3"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  SHAREHOLDERS SHARING AN ADDRESS    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;One copy of this 
information statement will be sent to shareholders who share an address, unless 
they have notified the Company that
they want to receive multiple packages. This practice, known as "householding," 
is designed to reduce duplicate mailings and save significant printing and 
postage costs. If you received a householded
mailing of this information statement and you would like to have additional 
copies mailed to you or you would like to opt out of this practice for future 
mailings, the Company will promptly deliver
such additional copies to you if you submit your request in writing to Clayton 
Williams Energy,&nbsp;Inc., Attn: Investor Relations, 6 Desta Drive, 
Suite&nbsp;6500, Midland, Texas&nbsp;79705, or
by contacting Investor Relations at (432)&nbsp;688-3419. In addition, 
shareholders sharing an address who are currently receiving multiple copies may 
also notify the Company at such address or phone
number if they wish to receive only a single copy. </FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="de17301_additional_information"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_de17301_4"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  ADDITIONAL INFORMATION    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If you would like to 
receive further information about Clayton Williams Energy,&nbsp;Inc., please 
visit the Company's website at
www.claytonwilliams.com. The "Investors" section of the Company's website 
contains, among other things, management presentations, financial information, 
stock quotes and links to the Company's filings
with the SEC. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In
this information statement, the Company states that information and documents 
are available on the Company's website. These references are merely intended to 
suggest where the
Company's shareholders may obtain additional information. The materials and 
other information presented on the Company's website are not incorporated in and
should not otherwise be considered part of
this information statement. </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="le17301_common_stock_purchase_agreement"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_le17301_1"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  COMMON STOCK PURCHASE AGREEMENT    <BR>    
</B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This COMMON STOCK 
PURCHASE AGREEMENT, dated as of July&nbsp;22, 2016 (this
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), is by and among 
CLAYTON WILLIAMS ENERGY,&nbsp;INC., a Delaware corporation (the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), and each of the 
purchasers listed on </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2> hereto (each a
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Purchaser</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" and collectively, the
"</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Purchasers</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
the Company desires to issue and sell to the Purchasers, and each Purchaser 
desires to purchase from the Company, certain shares of the Company's common 
stock, par value $0.10
per share (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Common Shares</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") 
in accordance with the provisions of this Agreement; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
at Closing (as defined below), the Company and the Purchasers will enter into a 
Stockholder Agreement (the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Stockholder
Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>") in the form attached hereto as </FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Exhibit&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>, pursuant to which the Company 
will provide the Purchasers with
certain board nomination rights with respect to the Common Shares acquired 
pursuant hereto and pursuant to which the Company and the Purchasers will make 
certain other agreements; </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, the board of
directors of the Company and the requisite holders of Preferred Stock (as 
defined below) have
approved an increase in the size of the board of directors of the Company from 
seven to nine directors, such increase to be effective as of the Closing; 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
the Company is party to that certain Credit Agreement dated as of March&nbsp;8, 
2016, among the Company, certain subsidiaries of the Company, as guarantors, 
certain affiliates
of the Purchasers and the other financial institutions party thereto from time 
to time, as lenders, and Wilmington Trust, National Association, as 
administrative agent (as amended by the certain
Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to Credit Agreement entered into on March&nbsp;15, 2016 and
as the same may be further amended, restated, amended and restated, supplemented
or otherwise modified from time to
time, the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Credit Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"); 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, the Company,
certain subsidiaries of the Company, as guarantors, certain affiliates of the 
Purchasers and the
other financial institutions party thereto from time to time, as lenders, and 
Wilmington Trust, National Association, as administrative agent, have entered
into an amendment to the Credit Agreement
(the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Credit Agreement Amendment</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>"), such amendment to be effective as of the Closing, pursuant to which 
the lenders agree to the consent and waiver of
certain matters relating to the use of proceeds from the transactions 
contemplated by this Agreement and certain other transactions; and </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;WHEREAS,
concurrent with the execution of this Agreement and in connection with the 
transactions contemplated by this Agreement, the Company has received a written 
consent delivered by
holders of a majority of the Common Shares of the Company irrevocably approving 
the transactions contemplated by this Agreement (the "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Company Stockholder
Approval</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOW
THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants and agreements set forth 
herein and for good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of 
which is hereby
acknowledged, the Company and each of the Purchasers, hereby agree as follows: 
</FONT></P>
<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><B> <A 
NAME="ARTICLE_I"></A>ARTICLE I<BR>
DEFINITIONS  </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="1.1"></A> </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="le17301_section_1.1_definitions."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_le17301_2"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;1.1</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Definitions. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As used in this Agreement, and unless the context
requires a different meaning,
 the following terms have the meanings indicated: </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Affiliate</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, with respect to any Person, 
any other Person that directly or indirectly through one or more intermediaries 
controls,
is controlled by or is under common control with, the Person in question. As 
used herein, the term "control" means the possession, direct or indirect, of the
power to direct or cause the direction of
the management and policies of a Person, whether through ownership of voting 
securities, by contract or otherwise. </FONT></P>
<HR NOSHADE>
<P style='font-family:times;page-break-before:always'></p>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Antitrust Laws</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, collectively, 
(a)&nbsp;the Hart-Scott-Rodino Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended; 
(b)&nbsp;the
Sherman Antitrust Act of 1890, as amended; (c)&nbsp;the Clayton Act of 1914, as 
amended; (d)&nbsp;the Federal Trade Commission Act of 1914, as amended; 
(e)&nbsp;any other applicable Law designed
to prohibit, restrict or regulate actions for the purpose or effect of 
monopolization or restraint of trade; and (f)&nbsp;any applicable Law that 
requires one or more parties to certain transactions
to submit notice or information to a Governmental Authority charged with 
enforcing any applicable Law identified in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>clause&nbsp;
(e)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> of this
definition. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Business Day</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any day other than a 
Saturday, Sunday, any federal legal holiday or day on which banking institutions
in the state of
New York are authorized or required by Law or other governmental action to 
close. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;2.2</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;2.2</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Commission</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means the United States Securities
and Exchange Commission. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in the 
introductory paragraph. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

SIZE=2><I>Company SEC Documents</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning 
specified in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.8</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Company Stockholder Approval</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning 
specified in the recitals. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Common Share Price</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means $29.6965. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

specified in the recitals. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>DGCL</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means the General Corporation Law of the
State of Delaware, as amended. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Environmental Laws</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified 
in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.10</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Exchange Act</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means the Securities Exchange 
Act of 1934 and the rules and regulations of the Commission promulgated 
thereunder. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>FCPA</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.13</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>GAAP</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.9</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Governmental Authority</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, with respect to
a particular Person, any country, state, county, city and political subdivision 
in which
such Person or such Person's Property is located or that exercises valid 
jurisdiction over any such Person or such Person's Property, and any court, 
agency, department, commission, board, bureau or
instrumentality of any of them and any monetary authority that exercises valid 
jurisdiction over any such Person or such Person's Property. Unless otherwise
specified, all references to Governmental
Authority herein with respect to the Company mean a Governmental Authority 
having jurisdiction over the Company, its Subsidiaries or any of their 
respective Properties. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Indemnified Party</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified 
in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;6.3</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

<A NAME="page_le17301_1_3"> </A>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Law</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any federal, state, local or 
foreign order, writ, injunction, judgment, settlement, award, decree, statute, 
law, rule or
regulation. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Lien</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any interest in Property securing 
an obligation owed to, or a claim by, a Person other than the owner of the 
Property,
whether such interest is based on the common law, statute or contract, and 
whether such obligation or claim is fixed or contingent, and including the lien 
or security interest arising from a mortgage,
encumbrance, pledge, security agreement, conditional sale or trust receipt or a 
lease, consignment or bailment for security purposes. For the purpose of this 
Agreement, a Person shall be deemed to be
the owner of any Property that it has acquired or holds subject to a conditional
sale agreement, or leases under a financing lease or other arrangement pursuant 
to which title to the Property has been
retained by or vested in some other Person in a transaction intended to create a
financing. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Losses</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;6.1</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Material Adverse Effect</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any change, 
event, development, circumstance, condition, occurrence or effect that,
individually or in the
aggregate, has a material adverse effect on the business, assets, liabilities, 
condition (financial or otherwise) or results of operations of the Company and 
its Subsidiaries, taken as a whole, but
none of the following changes, events, developments, conditions,
occurrences or effects (either alone or in combination) will be taken into 
account for purposes of determining whether a Material Adverse Effect has 
occurred: (a)&nbsp;changes in the general
economic, financial, credit or securities markets (b)&nbsp;changes in general 
economic conditions in the oil and gas exploration and production industry as a 
result of changes in the price of oil or
natural gas; (c)&nbsp;the outbreak or escalation of hostilities involving the 
United States, the declaration by the United States of a national emergency or 
war or the occurrence of any other
calamity or crisis, including acts of terrorism; (d)&nbsp;any hurricane, 
tornado, flood, earthquake or other natural disaster or any pandemic; 
(e)&nbsp;any changes in accounting requirements or
principles imposed upon the Company and its Subsidiaries or their respective 
businesses or any changes in GAAP (or authoritative interpretation of GAAP); 
(f)&nbsp;any change in the market price or
trading volume of the Common Shares (it being understood and agreed that the 
exception in this clause&nbsp;(f) shall not preclude any Party from asserting 
that the facts, circumstances, changes,
events, developments, conditions, occurrences or effects giving rise to such 
change should be deemed to constitute, or be taken into account in determining 
whether there has been a Material Adverse
Effect); and (g)&nbsp;changes in any Laws or regulations applicable to the 
Company or its Subsidiaries or the industries in which they operates or the 
interpretations thereof; </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>provided</I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>, </FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>however</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>, that any change, event, development, 
circumstance, condition, occurrence or effect
referred to in clauses&nbsp;(a), (b), (c), (d)&nbsp;or (g)&nbsp;will be taken 
into account for purposes of determining whether a Material Adverse Effect has 
occurred if and to the extent that
such change, event, development, circumstance, condition, occurrence or effect 
disproportionately affects the Company and its Subsidiaries, taken as a whole, 
as compared to other similarly situated
Persons operating in the industries in which the Company and its Subsidiaries 
operate. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Money Laundering Laws</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning 
specified in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.14</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>NYSE</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means The New York Stock 
Exchange,&nbsp;Inc. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>OFAC</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;3.15</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Operative Documents</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, collectively, this
Agreement and the Stockholder Agreement, and any amendments, supplements, 
continuations or
modifications thereto. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Outside Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;7.9(b)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Person</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means an individual or a corporation, 
limited liability company, partnership, joint venture, trust, unincorporated 
organization,
association, government agency or political subdivision thereof or other form of
entity. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Press Release</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning specified in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;5.1(b)</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Property</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means any interest in any kind of 
property or asset, whether real, personal or mixed, or tangible or intangible. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Purchase Price</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, with respect to a 
particular Purchaser, the portion of the aggregate amount set forth on </FONT> 
<FONT SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> hereto under the column 
titled "Purchase
Price" set forth opposite such Purchaser's name on the Allocation Schedule. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Purchased Shares</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, with respect to a 
particular Purchaser, the portion of the aggregate number of Common Shares set 
forth on </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> hereto 
under the
column titled "Aggregate Shares of Common Stock" opposite such Purchaser's name 
on the Allocation Schedule. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Purchaser</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" and "</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Purchasers</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" have the meanings specified in the
introductory paragraph. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Purchaser Related Parties</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" has the meaning 
specified in </FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Section&nbsp;6.1</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Registration Rights Agreement</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means that 
certain Registration Rights Agreement, dated March&nbsp;15, 2016, between the 
Company and the
sellers listed on Schedule&nbsp;I attached thereto. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Representatives</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" of any Person means the 
Affiliates, officers, directors, managers, employees, agents, counsel, 
accountants, investment
bankers, investment advisers and other representatives of such Person. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Securities Act</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means the Securities Act of 
1933 and the rules and regulations of the Commission promulgated thereunder. 
</FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Short Sales</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>" means, without limitation, all 
"short sales" as defined in Rule&nbsp;200 promulgated under Regulation SHO under
the
Exchange Act, whether or not against the box, and forward sale contracts, 
options, puts, calls, short sales, "put equivalent positions" (as defined in 
Rule&nbsp;16a-1(h) under the Exchange Act) and
similar arrangements, and sales and other transactions through non-U.S. broker 
dealers or foreign regulated brokers. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;"</FONT><FONT

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;2.1</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Sale and Purchase. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the terms and conditions hereof, the 
Company hereby agrees to
issue and sell to the Purchasers and each Purchaser hereby agrees to purchase 
from the
Company, its respective Purchased Shares, and each Purchaser agrees to pay the 
Company the Common Share Price for each Purchased Share. </FONT></P>

the offices of Vinson&nbsp;&amp; Elkins&nbsp;L.L.P., 2801 Via Fortuna, 
Suite&nbsp;100, Austin, Texas 78746 at
9:00&nbsp;a.m. (Central Time) on the date that all conditions set forth in 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Sections&nbsp;2.3</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> and 
</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>2.4</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>
have been satisfied or waived (other than those conditions that by their nature 
are to be satisfied by actions taken at Closing), or at such other time as the 
Company and Purchasers representing a
majority of the aggregate Purchase Prices determine (the date of such closing, 
the "</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Closing Date</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"). At least two
Business Days prior to the Closing
Date, the Purchasers shall deliver to the Company a schedule setting forth, with
respect to a particular Purchaser, (a)&nbsp;the portion of the aggregate amount 
set forth on </FONT> <FONT SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;A</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> 
hereto under
the </FONT></P>

<P ALIGN="CENTER" style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="le17301_article_iii_representa__le102377"> </A>
<A NAME="toc_le17301_9"> </A>
<BR></FONT><FONT SIZE=2><B>  ARTICLE III<BR>  <BR>    REPRESENTATIONS AND 
WARRANTIES OF THE COMPANY    <BR>    </B></FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company represents 
and warrants to each Purchaser as follows: </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="le17301_section_3.1_existence."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_le17301_10"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.1</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Existence. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has been duly incorporated and is 
existing and in good standing
under the laws of the State of Delaware, with corporate power and authority to 
own its
properties and conduct the businesses in which it is currently engaged and the 
Company is duly qualified to do business as a foreign corporation in good 
standing in all other jurisdictions in which
its ownership or lease of property or the conduct of its business requires such 
qualification, except where the failure to be duly qualified or in good standing
would not, individually or in the
aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.2_capitalization."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_1"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.2</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Capitalization. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
authorized capital stock of the Company consists of (i)&nbsp;3,000,000 shares of
preferred stock, par value $0.10 per share ("</FONT><FONT SIZE=2><I>Preferred
Stock</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2>"), and (ii)&nbsp;30,000,000 shares of Common 
Shares. As of the close of business on July&nbsp;22, 2016, there were 
(i)&nbsp;3,500 shares of Preferred Stock
outstanding and (ii)&nbsp;12,169,536 shares of Common Shares outstanding. All 
issued and outstanding shares of Preferred Stock and Common Shares have been 
duly authorized and validly issued and are
fully paid and nonassessable. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As
of the close of business on July&nbsp;22, 2016, the Company has reserved an 
aggregate of 1,400,000 shares of Common Shares for issuance pursuant to the 
Company's
Long-Term Incentive Plan, under which (i)&nbsp;no shares have been issued and 
are reflected in the currently outstanding Common Shares, and 
(ii)&nbsp;1,400,000 shares remain available for future
grant. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As
of the close of business on July&nbsp;22, 2016, the Company has authorized and 
reserved for issuance an aggregate of 2,251,364 shares of Common Shares pursuant
to
the exercise of warrants granted to funds managed by Ares Management,&nbsp;L.P.,
as further disclosed in the Company SEC Documents. </FONT></P>
</UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.3_subsidiaries."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_2"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.3</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subsidiaries. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As of the date hereof, the entities listed on 
</FONT><FONT
SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;B</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> hereto are the only direct or 
indirect
Subsidiaries of the Company. As of the date hereof, each such Subsidiary has 
been duly incorporated or formed and is existing and in good standing under the 
laws of the jurisdiction of its
incorporation or formation, with corporate, limited liability company, limited 
partnership, or other similar power and authority to own its properties and 
conduct businesses in which it is currently
engaged; and each Subsidiary listed on </FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>Schedule&nbsp;B</I></FONT><FONT SIZE=2> hereto is duly qualified to do
business as a foreign corporation or other entity in good
standing in all other jurisdictions in which its ownership or lease of property 
or the conduct of its business requires such qualification, except where the 
failure to be duly qualified or in good
standing would not, individually or in the aggregate, have a Material Adverse 
Effect; all of the issued and outstanding capital stock or other ownership 
interests of each such Subsidiary has been duly
authorized and validly issued and, in the case of any such corporation, is fully
paid and nonassessable; and the capital stock or other ownership interests of 
each such Subsidiary owned by the
Company, directly or indirectly, is owned free from liens, encumbrances and 
defects, except for Liens pursuant to credit agreements and related security 
agreements disclosed or referred to in the
Company SEC Documents, or as otherwise would not individually or in the 
aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.4_no_conflict."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_3"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.4</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No Conflict. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth on Schedule&nbsp;3.4, the 
execution, delivery and
performance of this Agreement and the issuance and sale of the Purchased Shares 
will not
result in a breach or violation of any of the terms and provisions of, or 
constitute, or with the giving of notice or lapse of time, would constitute, a 
default under, or result in the imposition of
any lien, charge or encumbrance upon any property or assets of the Company or 
any of its Subsidiaries pursuant to, (i)&nbsp;their respective certificate of 
formation, limited liability company
agreement, limited partnership agreement, charter, or by-laws or similar 
organizational documents of the Company or any of its Subsidiaries, 
(ii)&nbsp;other than the expiration or termination of any
applicable waiting period under the Antitrust Laws, any statute, rule, 
regulation or order of any governmental agency or body or any court, domestic or
foreign, having jurisdiction over the Company or
any of its Subsidiaries or any of their properties, or (iii)&nbsp;any agreement 
or instrument to which the Company or any of its Subsidiaries is a party or by 
which the Company or any of its
Subsidiaries is bound or to which any of the properties of the Company or any of
its Subsidiaries is subject, except in the case of clauses&nbsp;(ii) and 
(iii)&nbsp;as would not reasonably be
expected to have a Material Adverse Effect. </FONT></P>

<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.5_authority."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_4"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.5</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Authority. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each
of the Operative Documents has been or will be validly executed and delivered by
the Company and, assuming due authorization, execution and delivery by each
Purchaser or its Affiliate, as applicable (if either such Purchaser or its 
Affiliate is a party thereto), constitutes, or will constitute, the
legal, valid and binding obligations of the Company enforceable in accordance 
with its terms, except as such enforceability may be limited by bankruptcy, 
insolvency, reorganization and other laws of
general applicability relating to or affecting creditors' rights and by general 
principles of equity. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
Purchased Shares have been duly authorized and, when the Purchased Shares have 
been delivered and paid for in accordance with this Agreement on the Closing 
Date,
such Purchased Shares will be validly issued, fully paid and nonassessable; the 
stockholders of the Company have no preemptive rights with respect to the 
Purchased Shares; and none of the outstanding
shares of capital stock of the Company have been issued in violation of any 
preemptive or similar rights of any security holder. Except as described or 
disclosed herein, in the Registration Rights
Agreement or in the Company SEC Documents there are no outstanding 
(A)&nbsp;securities or obligations of the Company convertible into or 
exchangeable for any capital stock of the Company,
(B)&nbsp;warrants, rights or options to subscribe for or purchase from the 
Company any such capital stock or any such convertible or exchangeable 
securities or obligations or (C)&nbsp;obligations
of the Company to register, issue or sell any shares of capital stock, any such 
convertible or exchangeable securities or obligations or any such warrants, 
rights or options. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The
holders of a majority of the Common Shares have irrevocably provided the Company
Stockholder Approval, and no additional stockholder approval or stockholder 
action
is necessary or required for the issuance of the Purchased Shares or the 
consummation of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, regardless of 
any subsequent transfer or disposition of Common
Shares; and the holders of the Common Shares that irrevocably provided the 
Company Stockholder Approval hold a majority of the Common Shares of the 
Company. </FONT></P>
</UL>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.6_approvals."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_5"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.6</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Approvals. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No consent, approval, authorization, or order of,
or filing or registration with,
 any person (including any governmental agency or body or any court) is required
to be obtained or made by the Company for the consummation of the transactions 
contemplated by this Agreement, except (i)&nbsp;such as have been obtained, 
(ii)&nbsp;where the failure of the
Company to obtain or make any such consent, approval, authorization, order, 
filing or registration would not reasonably be expected to have a Material 
Adverse Effect, (iii)&nbsp;such as have been
made or as may be required under state or foreign securities or "Blue Sky" laws,
(iv)&nbsp;the approval for listing on the NYSE of the Purchased Shares, 
(v)&nbsp;the filing with the Commission of
such reports under the Exchange Act or the Securities Act as may be required in 
connection with this Agreement and the transactions contemplated by this 
Agreement, including the Information Statement
and (vi)&nbsp;the filing of approvals, waivers or consents under Antitrust Laws,
and the expiration or termination of the applicable waiting periods thereunder, 
if necessary. </FONT></P>
<P style="font-family:times;"><FONT SIZE=2><A
NAME="lg17301_section_3.7_compliance_with_laws."> </A>
<A NAME="toc_lg17301_6"> </A>
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section&nbsp;3.7</FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2><I>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Compliance with Laws. </I></FONT><FONT 
SIZE=2>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Neither the Company nor any of its Subsidiaries 
is in violation of
any Law applicable to the Company or its Subsidiaries, except as would not, 
individually or in
the aggregate, have a Material Adverse Effect. The Company and its Subsidiaries 
possess all certificates, authorizations and permits issued by the appropriate 
regulatory authorities necessary to
conduct their respective businesses, except where the failure to possess such 
certificates, authorizations or permits would not, individually or in the 
aggregate, have a Material Adverse Effect, and
neither the Company nor any such Subsidiary has received any notice of 
proceedings relating to the revocation or modification of any such certificate, 
authorization or permit, except where such
potential revocation or modification would not, individually or in the 
aggregate, have a Material Adverse Effect. </FONT></P>
